 is din mahabharat se judi shashti devi kii katha bhi suni jaati he, jo is prakaar se he
 
 
 The beginning of the Mahabharata period
 
 
 ek anya manyata ke anusaar chhath parv kii shuruyaat mahabharat kaal main hui thi
 First Sun son Karna started worshiping Sun God
 karn bhagwaan surya kaa param bhakt tha
 He would stand up in the waist for hours every day and offer arrogance to the sun
 surya kii kripaase hi vah mahaan yoddha bana tha
 Even today, this method of arghya donation is prevalent in Chhath
 chhath parv ke sandarbh main ek katha yah bhi he ki jab pandav apana sara rajpaat jue main haar gaye, tab draupadi ne chhath vrath rakhaa

 lok parampara ke anusaar surya dev or chhathi maiya kaa gaharaa sambandh he

 uttar bharat main mahaparv chhath dhoomdhaam se manaaya jaataa he lekin ranchi main chhath puja kaa khaas mahatv he

 darasal manyata he ki isi sote ke paas draupadi suryopasna kiya karti thi or surya ko arghya bhi diya karti thi
 It is believed that the Pandavas stayed in this area of jharkhand for a long time during their exile
 kehete hai ki ek baar jab pandavon ko pyaas lagi or dur-dur tak pani nahin mila tab draupadi ke kehane par arjuna ne jameen main tir markar pani nikaala tha
 It is also believed that near this spring, Draupadi used to offer Arghya to the Sun
 surya kii upasna ki vajah se pandavo par hameshaa surya kaa aashirwad bana rahaa

 yah khulaasa 1,600 college students par unke fasebuk vyavhaar ke study par kiye gaye research main hua he
